Source Code

These source-code files were derived originally from the scan from MIT's Dibner Institute's now-discontinued website titled "History of Recent Science and Technology". It is believed that the original listing was preserved by AGC developer Don Eyles, copied/reduced by AGC developer Hugh Blair-Smith, passed by AGC developer James Kernan to collector David Craig, scanned by Gary Neff, and then passed to the Dibner Institute where unfortunately the high-quality scans were reduced in legibility as part of the online-presentation process, and the original scans discarded. The source code was transcribed from those images by Ron Burkey. The images from the Dibner Institute website, and unfortunately not the discarded original high-quality scans, though with a few high-quality replacement scans provided directly by Gary Neff, are now available at the Virtual AGC project website. Report any conversion errors to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 131 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-091
	17:53 DEC. 19, 1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

020841,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
020842,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
020843,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary 1C, revision 131.
020844,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
020845,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13 and Apollo 14.
020846,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
020847,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
020848,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the 
020849,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
020850,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 501-623 of 1729.pdf.
020851,000012:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
020852,000013:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
020853,000014:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 05/15/03 RSB.   Began transcribing.
020854,000015:                                                                                                  ##              12/01/03 RSB.   Entered/corrected the previously-missing code from
020855,000016:                                                                                                  ##                              the bottom of p. 595 using a replacement scan
020856,000017:                                                                                                  ##                              provided by Gary Neff.
020857,000018:                                                                                                  ##              05/14/05 RSB    Corrected website reference above.
020858,000019:                                                                                                  ##              2010-10-25 JL   Fixed p583 page number.
020859,000020:                                                                                                  ##              2011-05-07 JL   Removed workarounds.

020862,000023:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
020863,000024: 
020864,000025:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020865,000026: 
020866,000027:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
020867,000028:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
020868,000029: 
020869,000030:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020870,000031: 
020871,000032:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
020872,000033:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
020873,000034:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
020874,000035:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
020875,000036: 
020876,000037:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
020877,000038: 
020878,000039:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
020879,000040: 
020880,000041:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
020881,000042: 
020882,000043:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
020883,000044:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
020884,000045:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
020885,000046:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
020886,000047:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
020887,000048:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
020888,000049:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
020889,000050:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
020890,000051:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
020891,000052:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
020892,000053: 
020893,000054:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
020894,000055: 
020895,000056:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS -- ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
020896,000057:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
020897,000058: 
020898,000059:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
020899,000060: 
020900,000061:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
020901,000062: 
020902,000063:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
020903,000064: 
020904,000065:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
020905,000066: 
020906,000067:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
020907,000068: 
020908,000069:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
020909,000070: 
020910,000071:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG
020911,000072: 
020912,000073:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
020913,000074: 
020914,000075:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS -- A,Q,L
020915,000076: 
020916,000077: 25,2073  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
020917,000078: 
020918,000079: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
020919,000080: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
020920,000081: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
020921,000082: 
020922,000083: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
020923,000084: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
020924,000085: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
020925,000086: 24,2000           05327        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG

021330,000491:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021331,000492: 
021332,000493:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021333,000494:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 3
021334,000495:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021335,000496: 
021336,000497:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021337,000498: 
021338,000499:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021339,000500:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRTACKING BEACON AT THE
021340,000501:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021341,000502:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS.
021342,000503: 
021343,000504:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
021344,000505: 
021345,000506:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021346,000507: 
021347,000508:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED --
021348,000509: 
021349,000510:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL                                        FLAGUP
021350,000511:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      ENDOFJOB
021351,000512:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)                     WAITLIST
021352,000513:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER                                        FINDVAC
021353,000514: 
021354,000515:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
021355,000516: 
021356,000517:                                                                                                  #        P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS -- ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021357,000518:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E

021419,000580:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021420,000581:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021421,000582: 
021422,000583:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
021423,000584:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021424,000585: 
021425,000586:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021426,000587: 
021427,000588:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021428,000589:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021429,000590: 
021430,000591:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
021431,000592: 
021432,000593:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021433,000594:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021434,000595: 
021435,000596:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED --
021436,000597: 
021437,000598:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021438,000599:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021439,000600:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021440,000601: 
021441,000602:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
021442,000603: 
021443,000604:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE, UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
021444,000605:                                                                                                  #        UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
021445,000606:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
021446,000607: 
021447,000608:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
021448,000609: 
021449,000610:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM
021450,000611:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
021451,000612: 
021452,000613:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021453,000614: 
021454,000615:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
021455,000616: 
021456,000617:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021457,000618: 
021458,000619:                                                                                                  #        SEE LSR22.1, LSR22.2, LSR22.3
021459,000620: 
021460,000621:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021461,000622: 
021462,000623:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
021463,000624: 
021464,000625:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

Page 517 

021639,000800:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021640,000801:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021641,000802: 
021642,000803:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
021643,000804:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021644,000805: 
021645,000806:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021646,000807: 
021647,000808:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021648,000809:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021649,000810: 
021650,000811:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
021651,000812: 
021652,000813:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021653,000814:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021654,000815: 
021655,000816:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED --
021656,000817: 
021657,000818:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021658,000819:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021659,000820:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021660,000821:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021661,000822: 
021662,000823:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021663,000824:                                                                                                  #        
021664,000825:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021665,000826:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021666,000827: 
021667,000828:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
021668,000829: 
021669,000830:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN'T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS --
021670,000831:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE: SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021671,000832:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021672,000833: 
021673,000834:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021674,000835: 
021675,000836:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021676,000837: 
021677,000838:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021678,000839: 
021679,000840:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021680,000841: 
021681,000842:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021682,000843: 
021683,000844:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021684,000845: 
021685,000846:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021686,000847: 
021687,000848:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRSESSM
021688,000849: 
021689,000850: 24,2675  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021690,000851: 24,2675                                           COUNT*   $$/R21                                
021691,000852: 24,2675           44736        R21LEM             CS       BIT14                                 #  REMOVE RR SELF TRACK ENABLE
021692,000853: 24,2676           00006                           EXTEND

021872,001033:

021949,001110:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
021950,001111:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021951,001112: 
021952,001113:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
021953,001114:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021954,001115: 
021955,001116:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021956,001117: 
021957,001118:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
021958,001119:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE TEH CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
021959,001120:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN IN SIDELOBE.
021960,001121: 
021961,001122:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
021962,001123: 
021963,001124:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
021964,001125:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
021965,001126:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
021966,001127:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
021967,001128: 
021968,001129:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021969,001130: 
021970,001131:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
021971,001132:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
021972,001133:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
021973,001134: 
021974,001135:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
021975,001136: 
021976,001137:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
021977,001138:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20)
021978,001139: 
021979,001140:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
021980,001141: 
021981,001142:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
021982,001143: 
021983,001144:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT --
021984,001145: 
021985,001146:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
021986,001147: 
021987,001148:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021988,001149: 
021989,001150:                                                                                                  #        SET INPUT FOR LSR24.1
021990,001151: 
021991,001152:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021992,001153: 
021993,001154:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
021994,001155: 
021995,001156: 24,3210  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD

022064,001225:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
022065,001226:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION

022293,001454:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: RRLIMCHK
022294,001455: 
022295,001456:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022296,001457: 
022297,001458:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022298,001459:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022299,001460:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022300,001461:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022301,001462:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022302,001463: 
022303,001464:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 -- THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022304,001465:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022305,001466:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022306,001467:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022307,001468: 
022308,001469:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 -- THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022309,001470:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022310,001471:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022311,001472:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022312,001473:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022313,001474: 
022314,001475:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022315,001476: 
022316,001477:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022317,001478:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022318,001479: 
022319,001480:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022320,001481: 
022321,001482:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022322,001483:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS -- UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022323,001484:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022324,001485: 
022325,001486:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:   MAGSUB
022326,001487: 
022327,001488:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:  NONE
022328,001489: 
022329,001490:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
022330,001491: 
022331,001492:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022332,001493:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022333,001494: 
022334,001495:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND

022377,001538:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: SETTRKF
022378,001539: 
022379,001540:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022380,001541: 
022381,001542:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.
022382,001543:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022383,001544:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022384,001545:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY:
022385,001546:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU'S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022386,001547:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022387,001548:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022388,001549:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022389,001550:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022390,001551:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022391,001552:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022392,001553:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF.  THEREFORE, THE
022393,001554:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURN ON IF:
022394,001555:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU'S NOT BEING ZEROED
022395,001556:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022396,001557:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022397,001558:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022398,001559:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022399,001560: 
022400,001561:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022401,001562: 
022402,001563:                                                                                                  #        L       TC      SETTRKF
022403,001564: 
022404,001565:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:  IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
022405,001566: 
022406,001567:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:  NONE
022407,001568: 
022408,001569:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  TRACKER FAIL LAMP
022409,001570: 
022410,001571:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022411,001572: 
022412,001573:    4564           34753        SETTRKF            CAF      BIT1                                  #  NO ACTION IF DURING LAMP TEST

022447,001608:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RRTURNON
022448,001609: 
022449,001610:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022450,001611: 
022451,001612:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WTIH
022452,001613:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROES TEH CDU'S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022453,001614:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022454,001615:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022455,001616:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022456,001617:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON'T
022457,001618:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022458,001619:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USEING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022459,001620:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022460,001621:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022461,001622:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022462,001623:                                                                                                  #        TC TASKOVER.
022463,001624: 
022464,001625:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER-ON (garbled)
022465,001626:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022466,001627:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022467,001628: 
022468,001629:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022469,001630: 
022470,001631:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022471,001632: 
022472,001633:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022473,001634: 
022474,001635:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
022475,001636:                                                                                                  #        
022476,001637:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022477,001638: 
022478,001639:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022479,001640: 
022480,001641:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)

022482,001643: 24,3256                                           BANK     24                                    
022483,001644: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022484,001645: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
022485,001646: 
022486,001647: 25,2073  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022487,001648: 25,2073                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB

022496,001657:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RRZEROSB
022497,001658: 
022498,001659:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022499,001660: 
022500,001661:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU'S,
022501,001662:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURN ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022502,001663:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022503,001664:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022504,001665:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022505,001666:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022506,001667:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU'S
022507,001668:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022508,001669:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022509,001670:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022510,001671:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022511,001672:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022512,001673:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022513,001674:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022514,001675:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022515,001676: 
022516,001677:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)

022521,001682:

022573,001734:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  DORREPOS
022574,001735: 
022575,001736:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022576,001737: 
022577,001738:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE TEH RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022578,001739:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INIITALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022579,001740:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022580,001741:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022581,001742:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022582,001743:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLOAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022583,001744:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022584,001745:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022585,001746:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022586,001747:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022587,001748:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022588,001749:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022589,001750:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022590,001751:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022591,001752:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022592,001753:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANFERRED TO
022593,001754:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022594,001755:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022595,001756:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022596,001757:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022597,001758:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022598,001759:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022599,001760: 
022600,001761:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022601,001762: 
022602,001763:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022603,001764:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022604,001765: 
022605,001766:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022606,001767: 
022607,001768:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022608,001769: 
022609,001770:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022610,001771:

022612,001773:

022614,001775: 
022615,001776:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022616,001777:

022666,001827:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  REMODE
022667,001828: 
022668,001829:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022669,001830: 
022670,001831:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022671,001832:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF TEH CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022672,001833:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, TEHN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022673,001834:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022674,001835:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022675,001836:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022676,001837:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022677,001838:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022678,001839:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022679,001840:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022680,001841:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022681,001842:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022682,001843:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022683,001844:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022684,001845:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022685,001846:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022686,001847:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022687,001848:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022688,001849:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022689,001850: 
022690,001851:                                                                                                  #  CALLIN SEQUENCE:
022691,001852: 
022692,001853:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022693,001854:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022694,001855:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022695,001856:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022696,001857: 
022697,001858:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INIITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022698,001859: 
022699,001860:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022700,001861: 
022701,001862:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
022702,001863: 
022703,001864:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONL, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
022704,001865: 
022705,001866:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
022706,001867: 
022707,001868:                                                                                                  #        NONE

022761,001922:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES:        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022762,001923: 
022763,001924:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022764,001925: 
022765,001926:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIT
022766,001927:                                                                                                  #        RRMANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
022767,001928:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022768,001929:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
022769,001930:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
022770,001931:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022771,001932:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022772,001933:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
022773,001934:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022774,001935:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
022775,001936:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022776,001937:                                                                                                  #        TRANFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022777,001938:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022778,001939:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
022779,001940: 
022780,001941:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022781,001942:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
022782,001943:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
022783,001944:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022784,001945:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022785,001946: 
022786,001947:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022787,001948: 
022788,001949:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
022789,001950: 
022790,001951:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
022791,001952: 
022792,001953:                                                                                                  #        FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RADMODES
022793,001954: 
022794,001955:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
022795,001956: 
022796,001957:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022797,001958: 
022798,001959:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
022799,001960: 
022800,001961:                                                                                                  #  EXIT: REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT -- RADMODES
022801,001962:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)
022802,001963:                                                                                                  #        L+1 (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)
022803,001964:

022853,002014:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RROUT
022854,002015: 
022855,002016:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022856,002017: 
022857,002018:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
022858,002019:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
022859,002020:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
022860,002021:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
022861,002022:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
022862,002023:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
022863,002024:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
022864,002025:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND TEH PRESENT STATE OF
022865,002026:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
022866,002027:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
022867,002028:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
022868,002029:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
022869,002030:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
022870,002031: 
022871,002032:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022872,002033:                                                                                                  #        
022873,002034:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
022874,002035:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
022875,002036: 
022876,002037:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQURIED:
022877,002038: 
022878,002039:                                                                                                  #        TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
022879,002040:                                                                                                  #        (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENAGLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
022880,002041: 
022881,002042:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
022882,002043: 
022883,002044:                                                                                                  #        MAGSUB
022884,002045:

022886,002047:

022963,002124:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RRDESSM
022964,002125: 
022965,002126:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022966,002127: 
022967,002128:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
022968,002129:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF-SIGHT (LOS VECTOR
022969,002130:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
022970,002131:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU'S ARE READ AND CONTROL
022971,002132:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
022972,002133:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE CORRDINATES (SEE STG MEMO 699)
022973,002134:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
022974,002135:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOT THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
022975,002136:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
022976,002137:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETUREN
022977,002138:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
022978,002139:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022979,002140:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
022980,002141:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMOES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
022981,002142:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
022982,002143:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
022983,002144:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
022984,002145:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
022985,002146:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
022986,002147:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
022987,002148:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
022988,002149:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
022989,002150: 
022990,002151:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022991,002152: 
022992,002153:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
022993,002154:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESM
022994,002155:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
022995,002156:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
022996,002157: 
022997,002158:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022998,002159: 
022999,002160:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023000,002161: 
023001,002162:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023002,002163: 
023003,002164:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023004,002165:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023005,002166: 
023006,002167:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
023007,002168: 
023008,002169:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023009,002170: 
023010,002171:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
023011,002172: 
023012,002173:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023013,002174:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLES ATTITUDE -- RETURNS
023014,002175:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)
023015,002176: 
023016,002177: 25,2404           43020        RRDESSM            STQ      CLEAR                                 
023017,002178: 25,2405           01112                                    DESRET

023053,002214:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  STARTDES
023054,002215: 
023055,002216:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023056,002217: 
023057,002218:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.
023058,002219:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.
023059,002220:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITON
023060,002221:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023061,002222:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023062,002223:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023063,002224:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023064,002225:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR TEH RR DATA GOO INBIT
023065,002226:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023066,002227:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023067,002228:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IT SET,
023068,002229:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023069,002230:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023070,002231:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITON OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023071,002232:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF TEH REPOSITON FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023072,002233:                                                                                                  #        WITH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023073,002234:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023074,002235:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023075,002236:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023076,002237:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WITH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF TEH CALLING PROGRAM.
023077,002238: 
023078,002239:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023079,002240: 
023080,002241:                                                                                                  #        FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
023081,002242: 
023082,002243:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023083,002244: 
023084,002245:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
023085,002246:

023087,002248:

023089,002250:

023091,002252: 
023092,002253:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES
