023227,002388:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  BEGDES
023228,002389: 
023229,002390:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023230,002391: 
023231,002392:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023232,002393:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023233,002394:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023234,002395:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023235,002396:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHRE
023236,002397:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023237,002398:                                                                                                  #        PRESETN, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023238,002399:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023239,002400:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESET, THE CONTINUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023240,002401:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, AN EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023241,002402:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BFORE
023242,002403:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023243,002404:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023244,002405:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023245,002406:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023246,002407:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023247,002408:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023248,002409:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023249,002410:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023250,002411:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023251,002412:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023252,002413:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EEXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023253,002414:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023254,002415:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023255,002416:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023256,002417: 
023257,002418:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023258,002419: 
023259,002420:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023260,002421:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023261,002422:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023262,002423: 
023263,002424:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023264,002425: 
023265,002426:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, FINDVAC
023266,002427: 
023267,002428:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:  DODES
023268,002429: 
023269,002430:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023270,002431:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023271,002432: 
023272,002433:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023273,002434:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE -- RADMODES BIT 10)
023274,002435:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)

023321,002482:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  DODES
023322,002483: 
023323,002484:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023324,002485: 
023325,002486:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023326,002487:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023327,002488:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023328,002489:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023329,002490:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS:
023330,002491:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023331,002492:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023332,002493:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023333,002494:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023334,002495:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY FO TEH COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023335,002496:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023336,002497:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023337,002498:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023338,002499:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023339,002500:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023340,002501:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023341,002502:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAT SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023342,002503:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOT COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023343,002504:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023344,002505:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITON
023345,002506:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023346,002507:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023347,002508:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023348,002509:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023349,002510:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023350,002511:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESETN, THE
023351,002512:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023352,002513:                                                                                                  #        CALLED.  IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, TEH RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023353,002514:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023354,002515:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023355,002516:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023356,002517:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023357,002518:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023358,002519:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023359,002520:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023360,002521:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023361,002522: 
023362,002523:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023363,002524: 
023364,002525:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023365,002526: 
023366,002527:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023367,002528:

023446,002607: 25,2732           74740                           MASK     BIT12                                 #  THE SHAFT COMMANDS IN MODE 2 SO THAT A

024186,003347:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024187,003348:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
024188,003349: 
024189,003350:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
024190,003351:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024191,003352:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024192,003353:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024193,003354:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024194,003355: 
024195,003356:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024196,003357: 
024197,003358:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024198,003359:                                                                                                  #        RRDOT           LPS20.1
024199,003360:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
024200,003361:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
024201,003362:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
024202,003363: 
024203,003364:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024204,003365: 
024205,003366:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024206,003367:                                                                                                  #        00001 -- ERROR EXIT 1 -- RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024207,003368:                                                                                                  #        00002 -- ERROR EXIT 2 -- RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024208,003369: 
024209,003370:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 -- COUNT NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024210,003371:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY RADARREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024211,003372: 
024212,003373:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC -- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) -- A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024213,003374:                                                                                                  #        RM -- THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED BY B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024214,003375: 
024215,003376:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024216,003377:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM -- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED BY B-7
024217,003378:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN -- THE RR TRUNNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024218,003379:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT -- RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024219,003380:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,ADG -- THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS
024220,003381:                                                                                                  #                MKTIME -- THE TIME OF THE RR READING, DP, IN CENTISECONDS
024221,003382: 
024222,003383:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024223,003384:                                                                                                  #        RNRAD, THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 580 

024225,003386:                                                                                                  #                1) RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
024226,003387:                                                                                                  #                2) RR RANGE RATE, SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
024227,003388:                                                                                                  #        THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX, CDUY, CDUZ, AND TIME1 AND TIME2
024228,003389: 
024229,003390:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  LRS22.1X, A, L, Q, PUSHLIST
024230,003391:

024359,003520:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME -- LRS22.2 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 2)
024360,003521:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE: 4-11-67
024361,003522: 
024362,003523:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
024363,003524:                                                                                                  #        (Yes, I know point #1 is missing.  It is missing from the program listing -- RSB 2003)
024364,003525:                                                                                                  #        2)  CHECKS IF THE RR LOS (I.E., THE RADAR BORESIGHT VECTOR) IS WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF THE LM +Z AXIS

024371,003532:

024380,003541: 
024381,003542:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS -- A,L,Q,MPAC -- PUSHLIST AND PUSHLOC ARE NOT CHANGED BY THIS ROUTINE

024411,003572:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME -- LSR22.3                               DATE -- 29 MAY 1967
024412,003573:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION -- P20-P25
024413,003574:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY -- DANFORTH                                   ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024414,003575: 
024415,003576:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
024416,003577:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS ADN DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024417,003578:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024418,003579:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024419,003580: 
024420,003581:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024421,003582:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024422,003583:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024423,003584:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024424,003585:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024425,003586:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024426,003587:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024427,003588: 
024428,003589:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024429,003590:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024430,003591:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RADARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024431,003592: 
024432,003593:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:
024433,003594:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024434,003595:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024435,003596:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024436,003597:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024437,003598:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024438,003599: 
024439,003600:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024440,003601:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024441,003602:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024442,003603:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024443,003604:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024444,003605:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024445,003606:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024446,003607:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024447,003608:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024448,003609:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024449,003610:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN ACG
024450,003611:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024451,003612:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024452,003613:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024453,003614:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024454,003615: 
024455,003616:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
024456,003617:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024457,003618:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

024459,003620:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T

024848,004009: 
024849,004010:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
024850,004011:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
024851,004012:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE BE-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
024852,004013:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY TEH RENDEZVOUS RADAR
024853,004014: 
024854,004015:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024855,004016:                                                                                                  #        INTSTALL        LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
024856,004017:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
024857,004018: 
024858,004019:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024859,004020:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024860,004021:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024861,004022:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
024862,004023:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024863,004024:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX

Page 594 

024865,004026: 
024866,004027:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED

024869,004030:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024870,004031:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29

024986,004147:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES THE RELATIVE POSITION VECTOR BETWEEN THE CSM
024987,004148:                                                                                                  #  AND THE LM, LEAVING THE UNIT VECTOR IN THE PUSHLIST AND MPAC AND THE
024988,004149:                                                                                                  #  MAGNITUDE IN 36D.
024989,004150: 
024990,004151: 26,3333           77201        GETULC             SETPD    VLOAD                                 
024991,004152: 26,3334           00001                                    0                                     
024992,004153: 26,3335           01645                                    DELTALEM                              
024993,004154: 26,3336           77754                           LXA,2                                          
024994,004155: 26,3337           03720                                    SCALSHFT                              #  LOAD X2 WITH SCALE SHIFT
024995,004156: 26,3340           53257                           VSR*     VAD                                   
024996,004157: 26,3341           57165                                    9D,2                                  #  SHIFT FOR EARTH/MOON SPHERE
024997,004158: 26,3342           01661                                    RCVLEM                                
024998,004159: 26,3343           53715                           PDVL     VSR*                                  
024999,004160: 26,3344           01573                                    DELTACSM                              
025000,004161: 26,3345           57165                                    9D,2                                  #  SHIFT FOR EARTH/MOON SPHERE
025001,004162: 26,3346           52255                           VAD      VSU                                   
025002,004163: 26,3347           01607                                    RCVCSM                                
025003,004164: 26,3350           41434                           RTB      PUSH                                  #  USE NORMUNIT TO PRESERVE ACCURACY
025004,004165: 26,3351           21725                                    NORMUNX1                              
025005,004166: 26,3352           17724                           STODL    ULC                                   
025006,004167: 26,3353           00045                                    36D                                   
025007,004168: 26,3354           77657                           SL*                                            #  ADJUST MAGNITUDE FROM NORMUNIT
025008,004169: 26,3355           20201                                    0,1                                   
025009,004170: 26,3356           24045                           STOVL    36D                                   #  ULC IN PD0 AND MPAC,RLC IN 36D
025010,004171: 26,3357           03724                                    ULC                                   
025011,004172: 26,3360           77616                           RVQ                                            
025012,004173: 
025013,004174:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
025014,004175: 
025015,004176:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTS SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY
025016,004177:                                                                                                  #  RXZ = (SQRT (1-SINTHETA**2))RLC
025017,004178:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025018,004179:                                                                                                  #        ULC IN ULC, PD0
025019,004180:                                                                                                  #        RLC IN PD36D
025020,004181:                                                                                                  #        SIN THETA IN SINTHETA AND PD6
025021,004182:                                                                                                  #        RXZ NORM IN RXZ (N IN X1)

025076,004237:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025077,004238:                                                                                                  #  MCD NO. 0                     BY P. VOLANTE, SDC              DATE 1-15-67
025078,004239: 
025079,004240:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025080,004241: 
025081,004242:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025082,004243:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN TEH RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025083,004244:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025084,004245:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025085,004246: 
025086,004247:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -- BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025087,004248: 
025088,004249:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025089,004250: 
025090,004251:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM
025091,004252:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC        RRDESSM
025092,004253:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
025093,004254:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
025094,004255:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
025095,004256: 
025096,004257:                                                                                                  #  EXIT -- TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025097,004258: 
025098,004259:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025099,004260: 
025100,004261:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD (SP) -- FOR DISPLAY IN R1 --   00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
025101,004262:                                                                                                  #                                                11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
025102,004263:                                                                                                  #        OMEGAD (SP)   -- FOR DISPLAY IN R2 --   ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGNT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
025103,004264: 
025104,004265:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025105,004266: 
025106,004267:                                                                                                  #        SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
025107,004268:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
025108,004269: 
025109,004270:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025110,004271: 
025111,004272:                                                                                                  #        RLMSRCH         UXVECT
025112,004273:                                                                                                  #        VXRLM           UYVECT
025113,004274:                                                                                                  #        LOSDESRD        NSRCHPNT
025114,004275:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD        OMEGAD
025115,004276:                                                                                                  #        MPAC            PUSHLIST
025116,004277: 
025117,004278: 26,3442                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
025118,004279: 26,3442           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO                                  
025119,004280: 26,3443           55736                           TS       NSRCHPNT                              #  SET SEARCH PATTERN POINT COUNTER TO ZERO
025120,004281: 26,3444           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
025121,004282: 26,3445           00006                           EXTEND

025329,004490:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025330,004491:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968
025331,004492: 
025332,004493:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025333,004494: 
025334,004495:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTES LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025335,004496:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025336,004497:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025337,004498:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025338,004499:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025339,004500:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025340,004501: 
025341,004502:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025342,004503: 
025343,004504:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025344,004505: 
025345,004506:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRPONLY
025346,004507:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025347,004508:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025348,004509:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025349,004510:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025350,004511:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025351,004512: 
025352,004513:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025353,004514: 
025354,004515:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025355,004516: 
025356,004517:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025357,004518:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025358,004519:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025359,004520:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025360,004521:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 605 

025362,004523: 
025363,004524:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025364,004525: 
025365,004526:                                                                                                  #        NCR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025366,004527:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025367,004528:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025368,004529:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025369,004530: 
025370,004531:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025371,004532: 
025372,004533:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 10)
025373,004534:                                                                                                  #        LOSSM           LOSVDT/4                (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
025374,004535:                                                                                                  #        SAVECDUT        OLDESFLG                (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
025375,004536:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        READRFLG
025376,004537: 
025377,004538:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
025378,004539: 
025379,004540:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
025380,004541: 
025381,004542:                                                                                                  #        INITIALIZING, IF RR IS FOUND TO BE IN MODE 1:  JOB R29REMOJ AND TASK REMODE:  ALWAYS: TASK PREPOS29.
025382,004543:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATING:  TASK BEGDES29 & JOB R29DODES.
025383,004544:                                                                                                  #        RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.
025384,004545: 
025385,004546: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
025386,004547: 33,2000                                           SETLOC   R29/SERV                              
025387,004548: 33,2000                                           BANK

025389,004550: 33,2045                                           COUNT*   $$/r29

025391,004552: 33,2045     5014               NR29&RDR           EQUALS   EBANK5

025485,004646:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS THAT THE DESIGNATION IS READY FOR NEW DATA.  SETTING LOSCMFLG MAKES IT GO AWAY SO SETUP29D CAN

025491,004652: 33,2143           52255                           VAD      VSU                                   #        AND ADD THE RESULT TO R(CSM) - R TO GET
025492,004653: 33,2144           01720                                    R(CSM)                                #        AN UP-TO-DATE LOS VECTOR IN SM AXES.

Page 610 

025558,004719:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025559,004720: 
025560,004721:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025561,004722:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025562,004723:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025563,004724:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025564,004725:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025565,004726: 
025566,004727:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025567,004728:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025568,004729: 
025569,004730: 32,2550                                           BANK     32                                    
025570,004731: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025571,004732: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025572,004733: 
025573,004734: 32,2550                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025574,004735: 32,2550  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025575,004736: 
025576,004737: 32,2550           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025577,004738: 32,2551           55106                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025578,004739: 32,2552           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025579,004740: 
025580,004741: 32,2553           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWO'S IN VECTOR LOOP.
025581,004742: 32,2554           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025582,004743: 32,2555           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025583,004744: 32,2556           12564                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025584,004745: 
025585,004746: 32,2557           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025586,004747: 32,2560           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025587,004748: 32,2561           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025588,004749: 32,2562           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025589,004750: 32,2563           21101                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025590,004751: 
025591,004752: 32,2564           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025592,004753: 32,2565           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025593,004754: 32,2566           31101                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
025594,004755: 32,2567           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025595,004756: 32,2570           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025596,004757: 32,2571           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025597,004758: 32,2572           12600                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025598,004759: 
025599,004760: 32,2573           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025600,004761: 32,2574           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025601,004762: 32,2575           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025602,004763: 32,2576           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025603,004764: 32,2577           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025604,004765: 
025605,004766: 32,2600           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q
